                       <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="301">
                        At our solar powered, eco-friendly home, you will enjoy a large private bedroom with a comfortable queen bed. The house is close to the Airport, Downtown Phoenix, and South Mountain Park. A great home base for any traveler!
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="302">
                        Our house is in a quiet neighborhood about 1 mile from South Mountain Park. Just 6 miles from downtown and 6 miles from Sky Harbor Airport! As fellow AirBnB budget travelers and SuperHosts, we have a pretty good idea of what makes for a pleasant stay. The large bedroom includes a very comfortable queen size bed from Tuft and Needle - The #1 rated mattress in the world. We'll also provide really comfy sheets, pillows, and towels to make your stay enjoyable. There is a ceiling fan and oscillating desktop fan to keep you cool and you can also control the air conditioning if you get too hot. There is also a nice desk/chair and fast wireless internet is available for you throughout the house. In your room we have bins for recycling, compost, and trash so we can help you have an eco-friendly stay. A large air-mattress is available if you need it. The bathroom is right next to your room. We have one other guest room that will share this bathroom with you if that room is also booked at the same time. The bathroom will alway be kept very clean for you. A hair dryer and iron/ board are also available. In the large kitchen, you are welcome to prepare a fancy meal or just enjoy a complimentary cup of tea or hot chocolate! We have ice cold filtered water through the refrigerator, a four burner gas stove, outdoor BBQ, and microwave -- pretty much anything you need to prepare a meal! The laundry room is available for your use. We have a front loading washer and gas dryer as well as an outdoor clothesline. Laundry detergent is provided complimentary for our guests. We are an Eco-friendly house: 63% of our electricity is produced on our roof by solar. We have eco-friendly bamboo floors. In our backyard we grow grapes, mexican limes, tomatoes, red onions, garlic, carrots, green onions, serranos, jalapenos, basil, cilantro, squash, lettuce, spinach, snap peas, arugula, chard, broccoli, mustard, cress, pak choi, melons, and more. Our chickens produce about 18 eggs per week. About 90% of our waste is recycled or composted. If you want to learn more about eco-friendly living, please ask! Nearby you can hike or mountain bike the many trails of South Mountain, learn to rappel at Rappel Arizona, get some great authentic Mexican food, and check out the wonderful Musical Instrument Museum. We have been to many places around AZ, so feel free to ask us for a recommendation! If you are going to be travelling around the Southwest after your time in Phoenix, we will be happy to store any large bags, bicycles, or sporting equipment you have! We also have some sports and camping equipment including backpacks, trekking poles, and water bottles that you can borrow during your stay. Want to explore the desert? You can rent one of four mountain bikes from our fleet. A Cannondale SM500 is $10/ day. Kona Blast is $15/ day. Opus Sonar is $15/ day. and the Kona Four is $20/ day. Ask for details and longer term rates. A car bike rack is also available for $4/ day. In our backyard, you can relax on the patio or in the hammock and be entertained by our three chickens. They lay fresh eggs everyday and if you'd like to try some they are available for $5/dz. This is a great location for runners, hikers, mountain bikers, and cyclists! We have flat dirt canal paths 2 minutes away that are great for a workout! South mountain trails that will challenge experienced mountain bikers are just 5-10 minutes away. The 16,000 acre park offers over a hundred miles of desert mountain trails! We have great weather from October until May. June to September gets a little warm... Long term guests are welcome! We've had several graduate students and business professionals stay with us for a few weeks or a month while they work at an internship or on a project.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="303">
                        The house is in a safe, middle-class neighborhood on a quiet street. We are just five minutes away from South Mountain Park - the largest city park in the United States (16,000 acres). There are more than 51 miles of trails for hiking and biking! By car: Sky Harbor Airport - 13 minutes Phoenix Convention Center - 10 minutes Arizona State University - 15 minutes University of Phoenix Stadium - 25 minutes Desert Botanical Gardens - 17 minutes Sedona, AZ - 2 hours Grand Canyon - 3.5 hours

                       <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="565">
                        Super comfortable, functional, retaining many of its historic characteristics with all the comforts of a new home. Central location near Banner Hospital and 2 miles from Chase Field, the Convention Center and all of downtown. 5 miles from airport.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="566">
                        This space was created with your needs in mind. It's Scandinavian simple: clean, utilitarian, bright, open, and foremost comfortable. From the comfy sofa, the super comfortable and spacious queen bed with luxury linens and towels, the spacious shower to the fully stocked kitchen - you'll likely have everything you need no matter how long your stay - days, weeks or months. Yeah - even the toilet paper is super. Yet, it is a historic home - from 1936 - and some of that character will shine through - plaster walls, wood windows, tall ceilings, brick exterior, funky layout and a porch are just some of the clues this home is from another century - all think you'll enjoy with while drinking French press coffee while waving to the neighbors walking their dog.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="567">
                        The Coronado Historic District is amongst the most vibrant and interesting neighborhoods in Phoenix. It's a people's hood. You'll see lots of people walking and riding bikes, interesting almost original homes and newly remodeled ones with lots of individual character. This hood continues to hit the top places to live lists in Phoenix, because its central location close to popular places to visit and go, within walking distance to local restaurants, and generally great vibe. Banner Hospital - walking distance Sky Harbor Airport 5 miles / 11 minutes Phoenix Convention Center 2 miles / 8 minutes ASU Downtown 1.7 Miles / 7 minutes ASU Tempe 10 miles / 16 minutes UofP Stadium 18 miles / 19 minutes

                      <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="705">
                       <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="706">
                        Phoenix is amazing this time of year! I can host larger groups and be creative with your needs and the space, just ask! The This turn of the century casita is loaded with eclectic charm. The neighborhood is unique,walking distance to galleries,restaurants and just a short jog to the convention center! You'll have a comfortable private bedroom with a king size bed &amp; bath. 2nd bedroom is available as well! I also have a vintage trailer that kids (or adults) could have a retro nights rest!
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="707">
                        Welcome to Phoenix and the Arts District Casita! This charming 1912 Phoenix bungalow has hardwood floors and tile throughout. You will have a master suite and, optionally, second a full size bed/art studio. There is a city-lights phoenix skyline view from the back yard and your window. From the front porch it's hard to imagine that you are in the heart of downtown Phoenix. This sweet tree lined neighborhood called, "the Triangle is vibrant and friendly. The Triangle is artsy with urban grit, authentic, steeped in the history of Phoenix. In the evening you might faintly hear, Japanese drumming from the karate studio four blocks away or a mariachi band practicing down the street and quite possibly my neighbors playing with their grandkids and joking in Spanish. The Hu-O-Te mini park is a 1/2 block away and is great for kids and critters. I teach a free 6:30 pm sunset yoga class there every Monday! I am sometimes out of town on weekends, so you may (or may not)have the whole house to yourselves! I can accomodate more that 4 persons but we'll have to talk about specific details before committing to additional persons. The space would be perfect if you or a small group is in town for workshops or a conference!
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="708">
                        This section of the arts district neighborhood is called the "Triangle", and is located between Roosevelt, 7th Ave and Grand Avenue in the heart of downtown Phoenix. It is a collection of historic homes and some new hipster-esqe condos. The Triangle is a historic, ethnically diverse, artistic, gritty, interesting neighborhood, and I couldn't imagine living anywhere else in Phoenix. There is a sweet little park a half block away, a great bar/restaurant with nightly live music called 3rd space only two blocks walk as well one of the best pizza joints in Phoenix! Great bars, cafes, coffee shops, galleries, and museums are very close!

                        <li data-reactid="873"><p data-reactid="874">Amy and Jason's place was honestly perfect! They we're so sweet and accommodating to us. The location was great, it was a short walking distance (or $5 uber ride) into downtown. Also a delicious coffee shop nearby called Cartel Coffee Lab and they made me one of the best cups of coffee I've ever had! The couch and bed were both extremely comfortable! The house was extremely clean and all of the furniture, bedding, etc. was brand new!                         Located in heart of downtown Phoenix guests have easy access to all of the amenities and attractions the city has to offer. Walk or bike within minutes to the Phoenix Convention Center, ASU, Comerica Theater, Talking Stick Arena, Roosevelt Row, the arts district, light rail, museums, galleries and much more.                        </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="1091">
                        This recently renovated one-bedroom apartment is conveniently located in the heart of downtown Phoenix. Features include a bedroom (queen size bed), living room with premium quality sofa bed (full size bed), single roll away bed (available upon request), fully appointed kitchen and private bathroom. Interior appointments include all new home furnishings, kitchen appliances, upgraded windows, flooring and rugs, bathroom fixtures and interior paint. Additional shared amenities include a pool area, semi-private outdoor patio, outdoor seating areas, barbecue grill, free WiFi, and washer/dryer access. Please note that we have several other suites available at this location for booking on Airbnb, as well as a variety of other accommodations in the Phoenix area (visit our profile page to review additional property listings). This property is conveniently located near the heart of downtown Phoenix with all of the arts and entertainment district amenities only a short walk or bike ride away. Popular nearby dining, arts and nightlife options include Crescent Ballroom, Valley Bar, The Vig, Phoenix Public Market, CIBO, Cobra Arcade Bar, Desoto Central Market, Roosevelt Row and much more. Less than ten minutes away from Sky Harbor International Airport (~$10 ride using Uber or Lyft). Keys to the property may be retrieved anytime after 3:00 pm using the lock box located near the exterior access gate on the south side of the property adjoining the onsite parking area. The lock box code for suite #101 will be provided prior to check-in. Overnight parking limited to one vehicle per suite. Guests with pets may be required to provide a security deposit. Please inquire and provide additional details prior to booking if you would like to bring a pet during your stay. As a courtesy to others, please remember to always clean up after your pet. Please contact us through the Airbnb app, call or text if you have any questions prior to your arrival. Also, please check out the downtown Phoenix guidebook found on our profile page for an updated list of all the exciting things to see and do in the area. Enjoy your stay! -Missy &amp; Matt
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="1092">
                        Honored with the first distinction of historical designation in the City of Phoenix, the Roosevelt Neighborhood has a storied past. From its architectural milestones still visible today, its importance in Phoenix’s original booming tourist trade, and its role as one of the first “streetcar suburbs,” Roosevelt has remained a vital community to our city’s past, present, and future. Today, as in the past, the Roosevelt Historic District is a thriving downtown Phoenix neighborhood characterized by diversity. Historically, it remains an important expression of the people and the building practices that established Phoenix as a progressive twentieth century city. The form of the neighborhood, the placement and arrangement of the buildings, and its distinctive landscaping all contribute to a character that reflects the economies, technology and popular tastes of a bygone era. Roosevelt is architecturally important as it displays a wide range of historic styles from the 1920s and 1930s that illustrate the changing architectural trends of the period. Residents enjoy easy access to all of the downtown Phoenix arts, sports and entertainment amenities, as well as easy freeway and light rail access to the surrounding metro areas.
                       </div>

                        <li data-reactid="1366"><p data-reactid="1367">Can I start out by saying how visually pleasing this place is? This place was decorated and put together with lots of tender love and care. A home away from home for sure. Upon arrival the place was spotless, very tidy. The living room had a tv with soundbar, no cable but we brought our amazon firestick and hooked it up to the tv and we were able to watch what we wanted. There is internet, which has a strong connection. The bathroom was stocked with ample towels, wash clothes, and hand towels along with hand soap, shampoo, conditioner, and a hair dryer (thank goodness). A ceiling fan right above the bed was also a plus, along with lots of closet space(URL HIDDEN) Aside from the place being beyond our expectations, the hosts were amazing! They were very accommodating and check in was an ease. The stopped in to make sure we had everything we needed and to show us where everything was. They offered suggestions on what there was to do around town, where the closest supermarkets were, where the parks were, where to rent bikes were, and lots of other great information. They were very flexible in working with us to figure out our length of stay, as we rebooked for a few extra days after being there for a previous week. Any time we needed to contact them, for whatever it was, they were quick to answer and very easy to reach. We would love to stay with these hosts again and most definitely would recommend this place to everyone and anyone!</p><span data-reactid="1368">Amanda</span><span data-reactid="1369">2017-01-06T00:00:00Z</span></li>

                       <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="1495">
                        My loft is close to Matt's Big Breakfast, Pizzeria Bianco, Hanny's, Chase Field, Talking Stick Arena, Welcome Diner, Lost Leaf, Monorchid Gallery , Symphony Hall &amp; Crescent Ballroom. In downtown Phoenix, on Roosevelt Row, it's easy walking distance to all downtown amenities - food, art galleries, entertainment. Inside enjoy the eucalyptus wood floors, gourmet kitchen, upgraded finishes everywhere and lofty high ceilings filled with natural light. Outside, swim, bbq and relax poolside!!!
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="1496">
                        The space consists of a large, 1000 Sq. Ft. 2nd story loft, that sits over a small Retail/Office and the Studio (Both are rented). Enter the foyer downstairs to the Studio and the Loft. A private stairway leads to to the space. It's basically one big open space (except Bathroom/Laundry - which is it's own private room), divided with furniture into distinct areas which all flow together. The kitchen area has a private balcony that overlook Roosevelt Row.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="1497">
                        Roosevelt Row is an Urban environment in transition. The University of Arizona and Arizona State University are both expanding their footprint in Downtown. This is brings a lot of activities, restaurants, clubs and diverse people to the Area. First Friday on Roosevelt Row is a big event, that includes Food Trucks, Galleries, bands and local artists.

                      <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="1735">
                       <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="1736">
                        Our home is comfy, clean, and relaxing. Located just 6 miles (15min) from the Phoenix Airport and downtown Phoenix (Convention Center) and only two miles away from South Mountain Park, we are a convenient location for both business and vacation travelers!
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="1737">
                        As fellow AirBnB budget travelers and SuperHosts, we have a pretty good idea of what makes for a pleasant stay. The blue room features a queen size plush pillow top bed. We'll also provide really comfy sheets, pillows, and towels to make your stay enjoyable. There is a ceiling fan to keep you cool and you can also control the air conditioning if you get too hot. Fast wireless internet is available throughout the house. In your room we have bins for recycling, compost, and trash so we can help you have an eco-friendly stay. The bathroom is very close to your room. We have one other guest room that will share this bathroom with you if that room is also booked at the same time. The bathroom will always be kept very clean for you. A hair dryer and iron/ board are also available - just ask! In the kitchen, you are welcome to prepare a fancy meal or just enjoy a complimentary cup of tea or hot chocolate! We have ice cold filtered water through the refrigerator, a four burner gas stove, outdoor BBQ, and microwave -- pretty much anything you need to prepare a meal! The laundry room is available for your use. We have a front loading washer and gas dryer as well as an outdoor clothesline. Laundry detergent is provided complimentary for our guests. We are an Eco-friendly house: 63% of our electricity is produced on our roof by solar. We have eco-friendly bamboo floors. In our backyard we grow grapes, mexican limes, tomatoes, red onions, garlic, carrots, green onions, serranos, jalapenos, basil, cilantro, squash, lettuce, spinach, snap peas, arugula, chard, broccoli, mustard, cress, pak choi, melons, and more. Our chickens produce about 18 eggs per week (in season). About 90% of our waste is recycled or composted. If you want to learn more about eco-friendly living, please ask! Nearby you can hike or mountain bike the many trails of South Mountain, learn to rappel at Rappel Arizona, get some great authentic Mexican food, and check out the wonderful Musical Instrument Museum. We have been to many places around AZ, so feel free to ask us for a recommendation! If you are going to be travelling around the Southwest after your time in Phoenix, we will be happy to store any large bags, bicycles, or sporting equipment you have! We also have some sports and camping equipment including backpacks, trekking poles, and water bottles that you can borrow during your stay. Want to explore the desert? You can rent one of four mountain bikes from our fleet. A Cannondale SM500 is $10/ day. Kona Blast is $15/ day. Opus Sonar is $15/ day. and the Kona Four is $20/ day. Ask for details and longer term rates. A car bike rack is also available for $4/ day. In our backyard, you can relax on the patio or in the hammock and be entertained by our three chickens. They lay fresh eggs everyday and if you'd like to try some they are available for $5/dz. This is a great location for runners, hikers, mountain bikers, and cyclists! We have flat dirt canal paths 2 minutes away that are great for a workout! South mountain trails that will challenge experienced mountain bikers are just 5-10 minutes away. The 16,000 acre park offers over a hundred miles of desert mountain trails! We have great weather from October until May. June to September gets a little warm... Long term guests are welcome! We've had several graduate students and business professionals stay with us for a few weeks or a month while they work at an internship or on a project.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="1738">
                        The house is in a safe, middle-class neighborhood on a quiet street. We are just five minutes away from South Mountain Park - the largest city park in the United States (16,000 acres). There are more than 51 miles of trails for hiking and biking! By car: Sky Harbor Airport - 13 minutes Phoenix Convention Center - 10 minutes Arizona State University - 15 minutes University of Phoenix Stadium - 25 minutes Desert Botanical Gardens - 17 minutes Sedona, AZ - 2 hours Grand Canyon - 3.5 hours
                       </div>

                       <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="1875">
                        303M is a private 1 bedroom unit with one of the largest private patios @ 300M. This is a small award winning redevelopment apartment complex. Now a modern sanctuary urban island truly in the heart of downtown Phoenix. Walk ability or a short uber ride to just about everything! cafes, convention center, stadiums, restaurants, museums &amp; night life. Home is 2 short blocks away from Roosevelt row ("arts district"). instant access to all expressways to get you anywhere in the valley.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="1876">
                        300M (300 E. Moreland st.) is Studio Darek's first redevelopment project. This one man against the odds project started after acquiring a 15 unit historic apartment complex in ruins located in downtown Phoenix, AZ., from the rubble it was turned into a modern and exclusive 9 unit living venue for individuals as unique as the space they seek to live in. In 2010 the same year it was open to the public 300M went to win The RED Award for Best Redevelopment; "Real Estate and Development Awards" are Arizona’s most comprehensive annual real estate awards. 300m has also been featured in a number of publications including Phoenix Magazine (2011) &amp; Arizona Republic (Jan. cover story, cool homes, 2012). Milk Bar is Studio Darek's most recent project added to the unique array of fantastic independent restaurants in this vibrant artist neighborhood. located a few blocks down the street. Where all 300mers and our guests are always welcome.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="1877">
                        We really are located in the center of all downtown phoenix has to offer! Hance park, Phoenix main public library, Phoenix center for the Arts is across the street. Phoenix Museum of Modern Art and the Light rail is 3 blocks west. Roosevelt row "Arts district" is 2 blocks south. where you will find everything from live shows, art galleries, restaurants, bars, cafes, music venues etc. 15 min walk to center of Downtown. Convention center is 1.25 miles away, both stadiums are about 1.5 miles away. Old town Scottsdale is about 20 mins away by uber. Roosevelt Row is known as one of the best art districts in America. It has a reputation for being very welcoming and fun, with many hidden gems. A few places that are local favorites are Milk Bar (also owned by the owner of 300M), Matt's Big Breakfast, Angles Trumpet, The Breadfruit and Rum Bar, and so many more! Just ask and we can direct you to great places to eat and drink. Don't forget to visit the Phoenix Museum of Modern Ar(URL HIDDEN)quick short cut walk across Hance Park. FYI Wednesdays free admission). Heritage Square for Phoenix history and tours as well as the Heard Museum to learn about the indigenous peoples of the area. With so many things to do not a moment will be dull.
                       </div>

                      <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="2295">
                       <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="2296">
                        Private Apartment with separate entry in Heart of downtown arts &amp; culture in beautiful Historic Willo district. Walking Score is 77!!! Walk 1 block to Central Avenue to Phoenix Art Center, Heard Museum, Light Rail 2 blocks &amp; numerous restaurants, coffee shops &amp; nightlife. Parking on street. Enjoy relaxing on any of 3 lovely patios. As your Hosts we provide lots of goodies to eat and drink and extra touches to make you comfortable and so, welcome home!
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="2297">
                        Home is in Historic Cottage Living district. This is a large 2 room apt in lower level of our home with high ceilings and an open feel, with full banks of window wells allowing great indirect light with shade cover &amp; private entry. 1st room has a full bed and the 2nd room has a full futon and features a completly outfitted kitchen including stove and oven so guests may cook. The apt. comfortably fits 4 who share sleeping. We can take more if necessary with discussion first as there's a blow up queen airbed. Extra charges per person apply over 2 guests, including children. There's a straight flight (14 steps) down to the apartment which are to code and have a sturdy handrail.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="2298">
                        Quiet, friendly, historic beauty. It is bike and walk friendly. We are centrally located in Phoenix art- focused areas with several theaters, museums, symphony &amp; opera. Walk or ride the light rail! Grid rental bikes available just down the street and there are designated paths through the neighborhood and into downtown &amp; throughout the Valley and Mountain trails. There are great places in walking distance to eat/drink including Starbucks, and from the light rail! ( our favorite place is Oven &amp; Vine one stop up on the Light Rail, or walking distance a few blocks!) Guests can take a short walk to the Phoenix Art Museum and the Heard Indian Art Museum (both have delightful lunch cafes!), to the Light Rail and Arizona Opera House, which has special offerings depending on the day. Talking Stick Arena with sports and concerts is just within 2 miles on the light rail with its own stop. The area is convenient to I-10, the 51 North, the 202 East and great for connecting to most Spring Training areas by freeway or Light Rail/metro transportation. Take a day trip to Northern AZ to see old mining towns like Jerome, or spend a day in red rocks in Sedona! Phoenix is a great launching place to take a trip to the Grand Canyon! And we'll keep the lights burning at home for your welcome back!
                       </div>

                       <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="2438">
                        Modern Urban Living for a southwest business or pleasure getaway. Convention center is 3 miles away. Enjoy D.I.Y.Breakfast. Have eggs in a "DASH" then go explore! Museums nearby, murals galore, Your brand new Tuft &amp; Needle Mattress will put you to sleep in a New York second. Cooking lessons now available!
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="2439">
                        Stay in a 1945 Historic home tucked into one of Phoenix Arizona's quirky, fun, historic neighborhoods in what Forbes magazine is calling a "Hipsterhood". The Coronado Neighborhood is quite eclectic and undergoing a revival. Modern artsy shared living space. For a small house it has a big feel. Contemporary eclectic furnishings. Rustic backyard. A perfect porch for enjoying your coffee. Say hello to Columbus, my Western Desert Box Turtle. He hibernates during the winter months. If you feel like doing some gardening you can make your own rock garden or help me plant a garden. Just thought I'd put that out there.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="2440">
                        So much good karma in this neighborhood. You will love the diversity of its people so get ready to embrace many different cultures while your here. This neighborhood is going through a revival! Take a walk to Indian Steele Park. Check out Roosevelt Row for First and Third Fridays. See the Phoenix Art Museum and The Heard Museum. Hop on a GRID bike or the light rail and explore. It's a great location to access most places quickly. Live music is a stone's throw away.

                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="2577">
                        Luxury Historic Home located near the heart of Downtown Phoenix. A great alternative to hotel living, this unique home is located 6 minutes from Sky Harbor Airport and within walking distance of the Phoenix Convention Center, Chase Field-home of the Diamondbacks, Talking Stick Arena-home of the Phoenix Suns, Arizona Science Center, Arizona State University Law, Arizona Cancer Center, Roosevelt Row, bars, restaurants, nightlife, and light rail transportation. Located in a quiet historic neighborhood, this charming home is surrounded by desert landscaping filled with fragrant flowers, plants, and fruit trees. This home is equipped with a full kitchen including gas stove, dishwasher, refrigerator, microwave, coffee maker, washer &amp; dryer, and all amenities. Relax and listen to the songbirds on the porch at sunset and BBQ in the private back yard equipped with comfortable patio furniture and BBQ surrounded by fruit trees and beautiful flowers. Comfortably sleeping four, this home will keep you wanting to stay longer (just let us know) or wanting to comeback for your next trip!
